# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="a0c42-102">.NET Framework 中的已过时成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a0c42-103">本文列出了 .NET Framework 4.5 和更高版本中已过时的类型成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a0c42-104">类型成员由程序集分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a0c42-105">本文未列出过时类型的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a0c42-106">有关过时类型的列表，请参阅[过时类型](obsolete-types.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="a0c42-1108">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-1108">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a0c42-1109">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe 程序集已从 .NET Framework 中删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-1109">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a0c42-1110">其所有类型和成员已过时，且在 .NET Framework 4.5 及更高版本中不受支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-1110">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in .NET Framework 4.5 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a0c42-1111">这些程序集过去用于承载 Windows 窗体控件和在 Internet Explorer 中运行可执行文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-1111">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a0c42-1112">该技术的替代项包括 ClickOnce、XAML 浏览器应用程序 (XBAP) 和 Microsoft Silverlight。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a0c42-1112">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
